================================================================================
        Data Preparation Workflow for Amplicon-Sequencing Projects              
                             Version 062022                                     
              Genetic Diversity Centre (GDC), ETH Zurich                        
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
The data preparation process is structured into distinct steps to optimize both 
memory usage and CPU efficiency within the HPC Euler (ETHZ) environment.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Overview: A - Data and Parameter Evaluation
          B - Data Filtering
              3'-End Trimming and Read Merging
          C - Primer Site Trimming (Amplicon Orientation)
          D - Primer Site Trimming
          E - Clustering
          F - Annotation
